I could only see the left side of him but I could clearly see what looked like a stun gun, extra mag case and cell phone.<br>\n<br>\nAs he passed I turned to see he was also open carrying a Glock. Then to my surprise the woman he was with was also open carrying a gun. I couldn't tell what it was other than a semi-auto. Normally I just shrug it off and go about my B-ness but then I thought of ya'll and how much a picture of this scene would be GT gold.\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"ctaFtFooterPage\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"ctaFtAuthorPage\"><a href=\"members/concretefuzzynuts.186289/\" class=\"username\" dir=\"auto\">concretefuzzynuts</a></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"ctaFtDatePage\"><span class=\"DateTime\" title=\"Aug 9, 2012 at 7:13 PM\">Aug 9, 2012</span></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a class=\"ctaFtReadMoreLinkPage\" href=\"threads/open-carry-in-the-grocery-store-pic.1436817/\">Read More</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"ctaFtRepliesPage\">Replies: 198</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\n\t\t</div>\n\t\n</li>\n\n\n\t\t\n\t\t\t<li id=\"featured-thread-1659551\" class=\"ctaFtBlockPage ctaFtBlockIconPage\" data-author=\"Truth&amp;Balance\">\n\t\n\t\n\t\t<span style=\"display: none\"><a href=\"members/truth-balance.239760/\" class=\"avatar Av239760m\" data-avatarhtml=\"true\"><img src=\"data/avatars/m/239/239760.jpg?1432899170\" width=\"96\" height=\"96\" alt=\"Truth&amp;Balance\"></a></span>\n\t\t\n\t\t\t<div class=\"sectionMain ctaFtContainerPage ctaFtBackgroundPage node_19\"><span class=\"helper\"></span>\n\t\t\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"hiddenResponsiveNarrow ctaFtIconPage\">\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t <a href=\"threads/get-your-coffee-just-another-boring-g26-gen4-range-report.1659551/\" class=\"Tooltip\" data-offsety=\"-188\"><img src=\"data/featured_threads/icons/1659/1659551.jpg?1492540537\" alt=\"Glock 26 -
